261→\tif !ok { // not gRPC error\n   262→\t\treturn err\n   263→\t}\n   264→\tev, ok := status.FromError(verr)\n   265→\tvar desc string\n   266→\tif ok {\n   267→\t\tdesc = ev.Message()\n   268→\t} else {\n   269→\t\tdesc = verr.Error()\n   270→\t}\n   271→\treturn EtcdError{code: ev.Code(), desc: desc}\n   272→}\n   273→\n   274→func ErrorDesc(err error) string {\n   275→\tif s, ok := This is\n// intended to allow passing through of specific statuses via the function set via WithRoutingErrorHandler\n// for the ServeMux constructor to handle edge cases which the standard mappings in HTTPStatusFromCode\n// are insufficient for.\n// If otherwise, it replies with http.StatusInternalServerError.\n//\n// The response body written by this function is a Status message marshaled by the Marshaler.\nfunc DefaultHTTPErrorHandler(ctx context.Context, mux *ServeMux, marshaler Marshaler, w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, err error) {\n\t// return Internal when Marshal failed\n\tconst fallback = `{\"code\": 13, \"message\": \"failed to marshal error message\"}`\n\tconst fallbackRewriter = `{\"code\": 13, \"message\": \"failed to rewrite error message\"}`\n\n\tvar customStatus *HTTPStatusError\n\tif errors.As(err, &customStatus) {\n\t\terr = customStatus.Err\n\t}\n\n\ts := status.Convert(err)\n\n\tw.Header().Del(\"Trailer\")\n\tw.Header().Del(\"Transfer-Encoding\")\n\n\trespRw, err := mux.forwardResponseRewriter(ctx, s.Proto())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tgrpclog.Errorf(\"Failed to rewrite error message %q: %v\", s, err)\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\tif _, err := io.WriteString(w, fallbackRewriter); err != nil {\n\t\t\tgrpclog.Errorf(\"Failed to write response: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tcontentType := marshaler.ContentType(respRw)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", contentType)\n\n\tif s.Code() == codes.Unauthenticated {\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"WWW-Authenticate\", s.Message())\n\t}\n\n\tbuf, merr := marshaler.Marshal(respRw)\n\tif merr != nil {\n\t\tgrpclog.Errorf(\"Failed to marshal error message %q: %v\", s, merr)\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\tif _, err := io.WriteString(w, fallback); err != nil {\n\t\t\tgrpclog.Errorf(\"Failed to write response: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tmd, ok := ServerMetadataFromContext(ctx)\n\tif ok {\n\t\thandleForwardResponseServerMetadata(w, mux, md)\n\n\t\t// RFC 7230 https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-4.1.2\n\t\t// Unless the request includes a TE header field indicating \"trailers\"\n\t\t// is acceptable, as described in Section 4.3, a server SHOULD NOT\n\t\t// generate trailer fields that it believes are necessary for the user\n\t\t// agent to receive.\n\t\tdoForwardTrailers := requestAcceptsTrailers(r)\n\n\t\tif doForwardTrailers {\n\t\t\thandleForwardResponseTrailerHeader(w, mux, md)\n\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Transfer-Encoding\", \"chunked\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tst := HTTPStatusFromCode(s.Code())\n\tif customStatus != nil {\n\t\tst = customStatus.HTTPStatus\n\t}\n\n\tw.WriteHeader(st)\n\tif _, err := w.Write(buf); err != nil {\n\t\tgrpclog.Errorf(\"Failed to write response: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tif ok && requestAcceptsTrailers(r) {\n\t\thandleForwardResponseTrailer(w, mux, md)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc DefaultStreamErrorHandler(_ context.Context, err error) *status.Status {\n\treturn status.Convert(err)\n}\n\n// DefaultRoutingErrorHandler is our default handler for routing errors.\n// By default http error codes mapped on the following error codes:\n//\n//\tNotFound -> grpc.NotFound\n//\tStatusBadRequest -> grpc.InvalidArgument\n//\tMethodNotAllowed -> grpc.Unimplemented\n//\tOther -> grpc.Internal, method is not expecting to be called for anything else\nfunc DefaultRoutingErrorHandler(ctx context.Context, mux *ServeMux, marshaler Marshaler, w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, httpStatus int) {\n\tsterr := status.Error(codes.Internal, \"Unexpected routing error\")\n\tswitch httpStatus {\n\tcase http.StatusBadRequest:\n\t\tsterr = status.Error(codes.InvalidArgument, http.StatusText(httpStatus))\n\tcase http.StatusMethodNotAllowed:\n\t\tsterr = status.Error(codes.Unimplemented, http.StatusText(httpStatus))\n\tcase http.StatusNotFound:\n\t\tsterr = status.Error(codes.NotFound, http.StatusText(httpStatus))\n\t}\n\tmux.errorHandler(ctx, mux, marshaler, w, r, sterr)\n}\n","numLines":205,"startLine":1,"totalLines":205}}}

implements comprehensive gRPC error status code creation in `api/v3rpc/rpctypes/error.go`. This file defines pre-constructed error variables using `status.Error()` with specific gRPC codes: `codes.NotFound` (ErrGRPCLeaseNotFound, ErrGRPCMemberNotFound), `codes.FailedPrecondition` (ErrGRPCLeaseExist, ErrGRPCMemberExist), `codes.InvalidArgument` (ErrGRPCEmptyKey, ErrGRPCInvalidSortOption), `codes.PermissionDenied` (ErrGRPCPermissionDenied), `codes.ResourceExhausted` (ErrGRPCRequestTooManyRequests, ErrGRPCNoSpace), `codes.Unavailable` (ErrGRPCTimeout, ErrGRPCNoLeader), and others. The Error() function converts errors between gRPC status format and EtcdError struct with Code() method. For HTTP translation, etcd uses gRPC gateway (`api/etcdserverpb/gw/rpc.pb.gw.go`) which automatically translates gRPC codes to HTTP status codes. The `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/interceptor.go` implements unary and stream interceptors that check for server capabilities and membership status, returning pre-defined errors from rpctypes when validation fails.\\n\\n## kubernetes/kubernetes\\nKubernetes uses multiple layers for error handling. The `pkg/kubelet/apis/grpc/ratelimit.go` defines ErrorLimitExceeded using `status.Error(codes.ResourceExhausted, ...)` and implements LimiterUnaryServerInterceptor to enforce rate limiting. For HTTP response translation, the gRPC gateway vendor library (`vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/errors.go`) provides HTTPStatusFromCode() function that maps gRPC codes to HTTP status: `codes.NotFound` → 404, `codes.InvalidArgument` → 400, `codes.PermissionDenied` → 403, `codes.Internal` → 500, etc. The DefaultHTTPErrorHandler uses status.Convert() to extract the gRPC code and map it. For API server error handling, `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/responsewriters/writers.go` implements ErrorNegotiated() which calls ErrorToAPIStatus() in `status.go`. ErrorToAPIStatus() converts any statusError interface (which StatusError in `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/errors/errors.go` implements) to metav1.Status with HTTP codes. The RequestScope.err() method in `rest.go` delegates to ErrorNegotiated for serialization.\\n\\n## grafana/grafana\\nGrafana's authorization service (`pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go`) creates gRPC status errors directly inline using `status.Error()` and `status.Errorf()` with codes: `codes.Internal`, `codes.InvalidArgument`, `codes.PermissionDenied`, `codes.NotFound`. Methods like Check() and BatchCheck() return these errors which propagate through the gRPC framework. The gRPC server infrastructure in `pkg/services/grpcserver/service.go` chains unary and stream interceptors including LoggingUnaryInterceptor and TracingStreamInterceptor from `pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/logging.go`. For Zanzana/OpenFGA authorization server (`pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/openfga_server.go`), errors are converted using `status.Convert()` and `status.FromError()` to work with the gRPC status package, maintaining compatibility with HTTP error translation via the gRPC gateway mechanism.\\n\\n## Common Pattern\\nAll three repositories follow the pattern: gRPC handler code creates `status.Error(code, message)` → gRPC server propagates to client → gRPC gateway or middleware translates gRPC codes to HTTP status codes using standardized mappings (NotFound→404, InvalidArgument→400, Internal→500, etc.). etcd uses explicit error definitions, Kubernetes uses multiple abstraction layers with StatusError interface, and Grafana creates errors inline during validation.\"\n}\n","numLines":200,"startLine":1,"totalLines":200}}}
